Subject: [dm-l] Call for Contributions: Early Career Researchers Online

we are pleased to announce that we will be hosting an online symposium for early career researchers of the digital humanities on the 9-10th of July 2020.
As many other workshops and conferences are being postponed or cancelled this summer, we hope to provide a forum for fruitful discussion and exchange.

We welcome short abstracts for project presentations as well as suggestions for round table discussions.
Submission deadline is the 8th of June.
For more details, please see the attached call for contributions.

Best regards,
Sven Kraus (Basel)
